##############
# GUI Events #
##############
add_namespace = ottomans_gui_events

country_event = { #Delete Irregular Divisions
	id = ottomans_gui_events.1

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_gui_events.1 option 1"
		clr_country_flag = created_irregular_template
		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Ottoman Irregulars" }
		every_state = { clr_state_flag = recruited_irregulars }
	}
}

country_event = { #cheat event for the AI (democratic path)
	id = ottomans_gui_events.3

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_gui_events.3 option 1"
		### Add Turkish Nationalist votes in favour
		add_to_variable = { nat_tur_sup_deputies = 30 tooltip = nat_tur_sup_tt }

		### Add Arab Nationalist votes in favour
		add_to_variable = { nat_ara_sup_deputies = 30 tooltip = nat_ara_sup_tt }

		### Add Conservative votes in favour
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCCON } }
			}
			add_to_variable = { con_sup_deputies = 30 tooltip = con_sup_tt }
		}

		### Calculate coalition strength
		OTT_calc_coalition_strength = yes

		### cheat for marlib path
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
				has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCLIB }
				NOT = { has_government = social_liberal }
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.15
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #firing revolts that already passed the threshold
	id = ottomans_gui_events.4

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_gui_events.4 option 1"
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				resistance > 70
			}
			OTT_launch_revolts = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Ottomans Turn the Tide
	id = ottomans_gui_events.5
	title = ottomans_gui_events.5.t
	desc = ottomans_gui_events.5.d

	picture = GFX_OTT_Ottoman_Revolution

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_ai = yes
		OR = {
			has_war_with = EGY
			has_war_with = PER
		}
		NOT = { any_enemy_country = { is_ai = no } }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_gui_events.5 option ottomans_gui_events.5.a"
		name = ottomans_gui_events.5.a
		add_ideas = OTT_Ottoman_Reinvigoration
		every_army_leader = {
			add_temporary_buff_to_units = {
				combat_breakthrough = 0.20
				org_damage_multiplier = -0.30
				str_damage_multiplier = -0.30
				days = 100
			}
		}
	}
}

add_namespace = ottomans_political_events

# Education Reform
country_event = {	#Education debate in the Meclis-i Mebusân
	id = ottomans_political_events.1
	title = ottomans_political_events.1.t
	desc = ottomans_political_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_OTT_Speech_Kemal

	trigger = {
		OTT_ottomans_have_post_defeat_content = no
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_political_events.1 option ottomans_political_events.1.a"
		name = ottomans_political_events.1.a
		add_political_power = 30
		country_event = { id = ottomans_political_events.2 days = 10 }
	}
}

country_event = {	#Medreses fight back against the OHF
	id = ottomans_political_events.2
	title = ottomans_political_events.2.t
	desc = ottomans_political_events.2.d
	picture = GFX_OTT_Kemal_Teaching

	trigger = {
		OTT_ottomans_have_post_defeat_content = no
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_political_events.2 option ottomans_political_events.2.a"
		name = ottomans_political_events.2.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_political_power = -10
	}
}

country_event = {	#Vote on the Education Decree
	id = ottomans_political_events.3
	title = ottomans_political_events.3.t
	desc = ottomans_political_events.3.d
	picture = GFX_OTT_Parliament

	trigger = {
		OTT_ottomans_have_post_defeat_content = no
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_political_events.3 option ottomans_political_events.3.a"
		name = ottomans_political_events.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ott_edu_passed.tt
		country_event = { id = ottomans_political_events.4 days = 1 }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_political_events.3 option ottomans_political_events.3.b"
		name = ottomans_political_events.3.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_ENDEAVOUR_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_ENDEAVOUR_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_NATPOP }
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		custom_effect_tooltip = ott_edu_refused.tt
		country_event = { id = ottomans_political_events.5 days = 1 }
	}
}

country_event = {	#Basis of the reformed code
	id = ottomans_political_events.7
	title = ottomans_political_events.7.t
	desc = ottomans_political_events.7.d

	picture = GFX_OTT_Desk_Kemal

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_political_events.7 option ottomans_political_events.7.a"
		name = ottomans_political_events.7.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottomans_political_events.8 days = 7 }
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SWI
			modifier = OTT_adopted_civil_code
		}
		add_political_power = 30
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = ott_institutionalised_islam }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = ott_institutionalised_islam
				add_idea = ott_institutionalised_islam_spd
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_political_events.7 option ottomans_political_events.7.b"
		name = ottomans_political_events.7.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottomans_political_events.8 days = 7 }
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = AUS
			modifier = OTT_adopted_civil_code
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 183 #Cyprus
					state = 339 #Smyrna
					state = 585 #Batumi
				}
			}
			ott_decrease_revolt_risk = yes
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 554 #Damascus
					state = 754 #Medina
					state = 995 #Homs
				}
			}
			ott_decrease_revolt_risk = yes
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 352 #Van
					state = 812 #Basra
					state = 819 #Sulaymaniyah
				}
			}
			ott_decrease_revolt_risk = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = ott_institutionalised_islam }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = ott_institutionalised_islam
				add_idea = ott_institutionalised_islam_spd
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_political_events.7 option ottomans_political_events.7.c"
		name = ottomans_political_events.7.c
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = OHF_tension_1 }
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ottomans_political_events.14 days = 2 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = reforms_blocked
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ottomans_political_events.8 days = 7 }
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.1
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { OTT_is_conservative_state = yes }
			ott_decrease_revolt_risk = yes
		}
	}
}

# Conservatives block the Kemalist Reforms
country_event = {	#Deadlock within the Meclis-i Mebusân
	id = ottomans_political_events.9
	title = ottomans_political_events.9.t
	desc = ottomans_political_events.9.d

	picture = GFX_OTT_Baghdad

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #New Elections Called
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_political_events.9 option ottomans_political_events.9.a"
		name = ottomans_political_events.9.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			country_event = { id = ottomans_political_events.18 days = 30 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ott_elections
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = OHF_tension_2 }
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ottomans_political_events.30 days = 10 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ottomans_political_events.18 days = 30 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {	#Elections of [GetYear]
	id = ottomans_political_events.18
	title = ottomans_political_events.18.t
	desc = ottomans_political_events.18.d

	picture = GFX_OTT_Sheikh_Islam

	is_triggered_only = yes

# Penal Code
country_event = {	#Status of the Alīye-i Emniyet Hizmeti
	id = ottomans_political_events.21
	title = ottomans_political_events.21.t
	desc = ottomans_political_events.21.d

	picture = GFX_OTT_Sublime_Porte1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_political_events.21 option ottomans_political_events.21.a"
		name = ottomans_political_events.21.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc_lar = yes
				has_intelligence_agency = yes
			}
			add_ideas = ott_reformed_secret_service_lar
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_anti_partisan } }
				upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_anti_partisan
				add_political_power = -100
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_psycho_warfare } }
				upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_psycho_warfare
				add_political_power = -100
			}
			else = {
				add_political_power = -75
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc_lar = yes
				has_intelligence_agency = no
			}
			add_political_power = -100
			add_ideas = ott_reformed_secret_service_lar
			create_intelligence_agency = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -75
			add_ideas = ott_reformed_secret_service
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottomans_political_events.22 days = 200 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_political_events.21 option ottomans_political_events.21.b"
		name = ottomans_political_events.21.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.025
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = OHF_tension_1
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = ottomans_political_events.14 days = 3 } }
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = ottomans_political_events.10 days = 3 } }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottomans_political_events.32 days = 200 }
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_OTT_Fevzi_Cakmak

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		has_government = authoritarian_democrat
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Fevzi loses
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_political_events.39 option ottomans_political_events.39.a"
		name = ottomans_political_events.39.a
		trigger = {
			is_in_coalition_with_social_liberal = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_ENDEAVOUR_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_ENDEAVOUR_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_NATPOP }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ott_elections
		country_event = { id = ottomans_political_events.40 days = 30 }
	}
	option = { #Fevzi wins
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_political_events.39 option ottomans_political_events.39.b"
		name = ottomans_political_events.39.b
		ai_chance = { base = 70 }
		activate_advisor = TUR_fevzi_cakmak_sic
		custom_effect_tooltip = ott_elections
		country_event = { id = ottomans_political_events.40 days = 30 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottomans_political_events.36 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

	desc = ottomans_political_events.41.d
	picture = GFX_OTT_Fevzi_Cakmak

	is_triggered_only = yes

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_political_events.41 option ottomans_political_events.41.a"
		name = ottomans_political_events.41.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no
			name = TUR_military_government
			long_name = TUR_military_government_long
		}
		end_coalition = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottomans_fevzi_events.1 days = 3 }
			country_event = { id = ottomans_fevzi_events.6 days = 14 }
			news_event = ottomans_news_events.3
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = EGY
						is_core_of = SUD
						is_core_of = ARM
						is_core_of = LBA
						is_core_of = TRP
						is_core_of = YEM
						is_core_of = HEJ
					}
				}
				clear_occupy_state = yes
			}
		}
		load_focus_tree = ottoman_fevzi_focus
		complete_national_focus = OTT_State_of_Emergency
	}
}

country_event = {	#Sheikh Seyid Riza declares Jihad
	id = ottomans_kemalist_events.33
	title = ottomans_kemalist_events.33.t
	desc = ottomans_kemalist_events.33.d

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OTT_ottomans_have_post_defeat_content = no
		any_state_of = {
			target = { 352 354 1000 } #Van, Erzurum, Kars
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = OTT_conservative_revolt
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 352 #Van
						state = 354 #Erzurum
						state = 1000 #Kars
					}
				}
				add_core_of = KDR
				transfer_state_to = KDR
				teleport_armies = { to_state = THIS.capital }
			}
			KDR = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = OTT
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { controls_state = 345 } #Sivas
				KDR = {
					set_province_controller = 3890
					set_province_controller = 7620
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { controls_state = 350 } #Diyarbekir
				KDR = {
					set_province_controller = 7530
					set_province_controller = 11739
					set_province_controller = 11759
					set_province_controller = 13745
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { KDR = { controls_state = 352 } } #Van
				set_province_controller = 4583
				set_province_controller = 12476
			}
			if = {
				limit = { KDR = { controls_state = 354 } } #Erzurum
				set_province_controller = 9858
				set_province_controller = 9868
				set_province_controller = 11853
			}
			if = {
				limit = { KDR = { controls_state = 1000 } } #Kars
				set_province_controller = 10472
				set_province_controller = 13672
			}
			KDR = {
				KDR_spawn_revolt_units = yes
				country_event = kurdistan_events.1
			}
			PER = { country_event = { id = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.44 days = 7 } }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_kemalist_events.33 option ottomans_kemalist_events.33.a"
		name = ottomans_kemalist_events.33.a
	}
}

				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		load_focus_tree = ottoman_endeavour_focus
		activate_advisor = TUR_ismet_inonu_sic
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_political_party = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0
		}
	}

country_event = {	#The Iraqi concession
	id = ottomans_economy_events.7
	title = ottomans_economy_events.7.t
	desc = ottomans_economy_events.7.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	picture = GFX_OTT_Al_Qurnah

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_economy_events.7 option ottomans_economy_events.7.a"
		name = ottomans_economy_events.7.a
		ai_chance = { base = 80 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = irq_sold
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = convoy
			amount = -50
		}
		OTT = {
			add_offsite_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 2
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = ottomans_economy_events.7.t
				category = excavation_tech
				uses = 1
				bonus = 0.5
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = convoy
				amount = 50
			}
			add_political_power = 50
			give_resource_rights = { receiver = ROOT state = 676 }
		}
		set_global_flag = irq_sold
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_economy_events.7 option ottomans_economy_events.7.b"
		name = ottomans_economy_events.7.b
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
		set_country_flag = irq_refused
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = irq_refused
					has_war_with = OTT
					tag = OTT
				}
				num_of_factories > 35
				is_subject = no
				has_socialist_government = no
				any_owned_state = {
					is_coastal = yes
				}
			}
			country_event = ottomans_economy_events.7
		}
	}
}

	id = ottomans_flavour_events.0
	title = ottomans_flavour_events.0.t
	desc = ottomans_flavour_events.0.d

	trigger = { #Avoidance for backup Lybia
		NOT = {
			tag = LBA
			is_subject = yes
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	# First on 15 December 1936, then reoccurs every 354 days
	# TRK, BUK, KHI, SAU, AFG, AZR, OMA, YEM
	# OTT and LBA get their own; ottomans_flavour_events.12
	# EGY gets egypt_events.200

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottomans_flavour_events.0 days = 354 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_flavour_events.0 option ottomans_flavour_events.0.a"
		name = ottomans_flavour_events.0.a
		add_political_power = 20
	}
}

	}

		name = ottomans_separatist_events.13.a
		ai_chance = { base = 65 }

			activate_decision = OTT_TRI_Fezzan_Expedition

				ott_decrease_revolt_risk = yes
				add_resistance_target = {
					amount = -25

					days = 250
					tooltip = OTT_resistance_garrisons
				}
			}
		}
		add_manpower = -10000
	}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OTT_has_centralist_government = yes
			}
		}
		273 = {
			ott_increase_revolt_risk = yes
		}
	}
}

				}
			}
			ARM = {
				ARM_initial_spawn_effect = yes
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ROOT
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			news_event = levant_crisis_news.9
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_separatist_events.35 option ottomans_separatist_events.35.a"
		name = ottomans_separatist_events.35.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_separatist_events.35 option ottomans_separatist_events.35.b"
		name = ottomans_separatist_events.35.b #Play as Armenia
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		ARM = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			PER = { country_event = { id = ottomans_separatist_events.36 days = 1 } }
			set_variable = { country_guide_page_count = 1 }
		}
	}

country_event = {	#Istanbul Pact - Invite
	id = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.18
	title = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.18.t
	desc = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.18.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_foreign_policy_events.18 option ottomans_foreign_policy_events.18.a"
		name = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.18.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { tag = MOR }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = MOR_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = MOR_forpol option = MOR_FORPOL_OTT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = MOR_forpol option = MOR_FORPOL_VICTOR } }
			}
		}
		##check if the tag has a guarantee from GER (in order to fix issue of AZR losing its guarantee upon joining and locking OTT focus)
		if = {
			limit = { is_guaranteed_by = GER }
			set_country_flag = OTT_for_temp_has_guarantee
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				add_to_faction = ROOT
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
				var:FROM.faction_leader = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
			}
		}
		#readd GER guarantee to tag if it had it before
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = OTT_for_temp_has_guarantee }
			GER = { give_guarantee = AZR }
			clr_country_flag = OTT_for_temp_has_guarantee
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_foreign_policy_events.18 option ottomans_foreign_policy_events.18.b"
		name = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.18.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				FROM = { tag = MOR }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = MOR_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = MOR_forpol option = MOR_FORPOL_OTT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = MOR_forpol option = MOR_FORPOL_VICTOR } }
			}
		}
		OTT = {
			country_event = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.19
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
}

country_event = {	#Ratification of the Sarajevo Accords
	id = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.24
	title = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.24.t
	desc = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.24.d
	timeout_days = 7

	trigger = {
		is_valid_peace_target = yes
		AUS = { is_valid_peace_target = yes }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_foreign_policy_events.24 option ottomans_foreign_policy_events.24.a"
		name = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.24.a
		set_country_flag = alliance_aus
		add_stability = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = { tag = OTT }
			complete_national_focus = OTT_Alliance_of_Convenience
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject = no
				OR = {
					tag = SER
					tag = MNT
					tag = ALB
					tag = ROM
					tag = BUL
					tag = GRE
				}
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = AUS
					has_war_with = OTT
				}
			}
			PREV = { give_guarantee = PREV }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {	#Meeting on Ada Kaleh
	id = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.26
	title = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.26.t
	desc = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.26.d

	trigger = {
		OTT = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = AUS
				is_in_faction = no
			}
			is_subject = no
		}
		AUS = { is_valid_peace_target = yes }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = AUS }
				if = {
					limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
					set_faction_name = faction_sarajevo_accords
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
					leave_faction = yes
					create_faction_from_template = { template = faction_template_donau_adriabund name = faction_sarajevo_accords }
				}
				else = {
					create_faction_from_template = { template = faction_template_donau_adriabund name = faction_sarajevo_accords }
				}
				every_other_country = {
					display_individual_scopes = yes
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = alliance_aus_accepted
							tag = OTT
						}
					}
					AUS = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { tag = OTT }
				complete_national_focus = OTT_Sarajevo_Accords
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_foreign_policy_events.26 option ottomans_foreign_policy_events.26.a"
		name = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.26.a
		if = {
			limit = { tag = AUS }
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = AUS_protector_of_the_balkans } }
					complete_national_focus = AUS_protector_of_the_balkans
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = OTT }
			effect_tooltip = { complete_national_focus = OTT_Sarajevo_Accords }
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_other_country = {
				display_individual_scopes = yes
				limit = { has_country_flag = alliance_aus_accepted }
				custom_effect_tooltip = OTT_add_country_to_sarajevo_accords
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = OTT_add_ottomans_to_sarajevo_accords
		if = {
			limit = {
				GRE = {
					is_in_faction_with = AUS
					has_country_flag = alliance_aus_accepted
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			TUR = {
				remove_state_core = 187
				remove_state_core = 164
				remove_state_claim = 989
				if = {
					limit = { GRE = { owns_state = 769 } }
					remove_state_claim = 769
				}
			}
			GRE = {
				transfer_state = 187
				transfer_state = 164
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {	#The Baku Conference
	id = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.56
	title = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.56.t
	desc = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.56.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference

	trigger = {
		OTT_russo_ottoman_convention_can_proceed = yes
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_foreign_policy_events.56 option ottomans_foreign_policy_events.56.a"
		name = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.56.a
		if = {
			limit = { #if Georgia is invalid, skip to Afghanistan
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = GEO }
					RUS = { has_war_with = GEO }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { #if Afghanistan is invalid, skip to Persia
					OR = {
						NOT = { country_exists = AFG }
						RUS = { is_ally_with = AFG }
						RUS = { has_war_with = AFG }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { tag = OTT }
					country_event = { id = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.66 days = 2 }
				}
				else = {
					effect_tooltip = {
						OTT = { country_event = { id = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.66 days = 2 } }
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { tag = RUS }
					country_event = { id = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.63 days = 2 }
				}
				else = {
					effect_tooltip = {
						RUS = { country_event = { id = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.63 days = 2 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { #if Georgia in alliance with Russia, skip to Batumi
				OR = {
					RUS = { is_ally_with = GEO }
					RUS = { has_guaranteed = GEO }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tag = RUS }
				country_event = { id = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.61 days = 2 }
			}
			else = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					RUS = { country_event = { id = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.61 days = 2 } }
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = RUS }
				country_event = { id = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.57 days = 2 }
			}
			else = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					RUS = { country_event = { id = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.57 days = 2 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.771
	title = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.771.t

	desc = {
		text = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.771.d.TUR_war
		trigger = {
			original_tag = TUR
			has_war_with = RUS
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.771.d.TUR_russia_dead
		trigger = {
			original_tag = TUR
			NOT = { has_war_with = RUS }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.771.d.RUS_war
		trigger = {
			original_tag = RUS
			has_war_with = TUR
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.771.d.RUS_turkey_dead
		trigger = {
			original_tag = RUS
			NOT = { has_war_with = TUR }
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = RUSSIAN_OTTOMAN_DEAL
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_foreign_policy_events.771 option ottomans_foreign_policy_events.771.a"
		name = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.771.a
		AZR = { remove_ideas = OTT_russo_ottoman_convention }
		RUS = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_guaranteed = OTT }
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = OTT
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = OTT }
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = OTT
					relation = non_aggression_pact
					active = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_military_access_to = OTT }
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = OTT
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { gives_military_access_to = OTT }
				OTT = {
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = ROOT
						relation = military_access
						active = no
					}
				}
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = befriend
				id = "OTT"
				value = -200
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = conquer
				id = "OTT"
				value = 200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = RUSSIAN_OTTOMAN_DEAL_AZR_BUFFER }
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = befriend
					id = "AZR"
					value = -200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = conquer
					id = "AZR"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = 266.ambition_area_@ROOT }
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = PER.core_states
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = ambition_area_@ROOT } }
					set_variable = { ambition_area_@ROOT = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		OTT = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = befriend
				id = "RUS"
				value = -200
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = conquer
				id = "RUS"
				value = 200
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = RUSSIAN_OTTOMAN_DEAL_AZR_BUFFER }
			AZR = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = befriend
					id = "RUS"
					value = -200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = conquer
					id = "RUS"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		OTT_clear_russo_ottoman_convention_effect = yes
	}
}

				country = ROOT

			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_foreign_policy_events.80 option ottomans_foreign_policy_events.80.b"

		RUS = {
			create_wargoal = {
				target = ROOT
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			GER = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		}
	}

country_event = {	#The Russo-Ottoman Convention
	id = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.83
	title = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.83.t
	desc = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.83.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = RUSSIAN_OTTOMAN_DEAL
		RUS = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
		OTT = {
			exists = yes
			is_subject = no
			has_capitulated = no
			NOT = { has_war_with = RUS }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_foreign_policy_events.83 option ottomans_foreign_policy_events.83.a"
		name = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.83.a
		### Persia
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = PER }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = RUSSIAN_OTTOMAN_DEAL_PER_SPLIT }
				413 = { #Khuzestan
					if = {
						limit = { owner = { is_ally_with = RUS } }
						transfer_state_to = OTT
					}
				}
				417 = { #Urmia
					if = {
						limit = { owner = { is_ally_with = RUS } }
						transfer_state_to = OTT
					}
				}
				419 = { #Tabriz
					if = {
						limit = { owner = { is_ally_with = RUS } }
						transfer_state_to = OTT
					}
				}
				421 = { #Kermanshah
					if = {
						limit = { owner = { is_ally_with = RUS } }
						transfer_state_to = OTT
					}
				}
				PER = {
					every_core_state = {
						limit = {
							owner = {
								OR = {
									is_ally_with = TUR
									is_ally_with = RUS
								}
							}
							NOT = { is_core_of = owner }
							NOT = { is_claimed_by = owner }
							NOT = { state = 413 } #Khuzestan
							NOT = { state = 417 } #Urmia
							NOT = { state = 419 } #Tabriz
							NOT = { state = 421 } #Kermanshah
						}
						transfer_state_to = PER
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				PER = {
					every_core_state = {
						limit = {
							owner = {
								OR = {
									is_ally_with = TUR
									is_ally_with = RUS
								}
							}
							NOT = { is_core_of = owner }
							NOT = { is_claimed_by = owner }
						}
						transfer_state_to = PER
					}
					add_ideas = generic_neutral_foreign_policy
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_socialist_government = yes
								has_government = national_populist
							}
						}
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
							elections_allowed = no
						}
						set_political_party = {
							ideology = authoritarian_democrat
							popularity = 60
						}
					}
				}
				OTT = { give_guarantee = PER }
				RUS = { give_guarantee = PER }
			}
		}
		### Azerbaijan
		else = {
			AZR = {
				every_core_state = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								is_ally_with = TUR
								is_ally_with = RUS
							}
						}
						NOT = { is_core_of = owner }
						NOT = { is_claimed_by = owner }
					}
					transfer_state_to = AZR
				}
				add_ideas = generic_neutral_foreign_policy
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_socialist_government = yes
							has_government = national_populist
						}
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					set_political_party = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						popularity = 60
					}
				}
			}
			OTT = { give_guarantee = PER }
			RUS = { give_guarantee = PER }
		}
	}
}

### Ottoman - Egyptian stalemate scripted peace
country_event = { #Peace with Egypt?
	id = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.96
	title = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.96.t
	desc = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.96.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_EGY_egyptian_palace

	trigger = {
		tag = OTT
		has_war_with = EGY
		is_valid_peace_target = yes

		#Egypt has lost initiative and has been pushed to the Suez
		EGY = {
			is_valid_peace_target = yes
			has_idea = EGY_levant_crisis_initiative_lost
			#All faction members in the Middle East have capitulated
			NOT = {
				any_allied_country = {
					is_in_middle_east = yes
					has_capitulated = no
				}
			}
			controls_state = 446 #Cairo
			NOT = { controls_state = 453 } #Sinai
			#Eastern bank of the Suez
			NOT = { controls_province = 1155 }
			NOT = { controls_province = 9947 }
		}

		#Ottomans are either under immediate threat, or too war-weary
		OR = {
			casualties_k > 250
			AND = {
				has_war_support < 0.2
				has_manpower < 10000
			}
			surrender_progress > 0.39
			AND = {
				owns_state = 773 #Constantinople
				NOT = { controls_state = 773 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_war_with = PER
				#OTT has been pushed out of Iraq and some
				NOT = { controls_state = 291 } #Baghdad
				NOT = { controls_state = 676 } #Mosul
				OR = {
					NOT = { controls_state = 350 } #Diyarbekir
					NOT = { controls_state = 352 } #Van
					NOT = { controls_state = 354 } #Erzurum
					NOT = { controls_state = 677 } #Aleppo
				}
			}
			var:global.russia = {
				at_war_with_or_justifying_wargoal_against_ROOT = yes
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = OTT_Union_Party_State } #Kadro-proofing
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Let's end this
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_foreign_policy_events.96 option ottomans_foreign_policy_events.96.a"
		name = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.96.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = OTT_EGY_scripted_peace_warning_tt
		EGY = { country_event = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.97 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = if_they_accept_tt
		event_option_tooltip = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.98.a
	}

	option = { #No chance
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_foreign_policy_events.96 option ottomans_foreign_policy_events.96.b"
		name = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.96.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}
}

			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_garrison_Nuri }
				remove_ideas = TUR_garrison_Nuri
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_garrison_Rustu }
				remove_ideas = TUR_garrison_Rustu
			}
			clr_country_flag = ott_egypt_garrison
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { OTT_anger_change = -1 }
			OTT_change_egyptian_anger_level = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		EGY = {
			add_stability = 0.2
		}
		set_country_flag = ott_armed_forces_reduced
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_foreign_policy_events.107 option ottomans_foreign_policy_events.107.b"
		name = ottomans_foreign_policy_events.107.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				set_temp_variable = { OTT_egyptian_anger_compare_var = 3 }
				OTT_egyptian_anger_check = no
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		set_temp_variable = { OTT_anger_change = 1 }
		OTT_change_egyptian_anger_level = yes
		EGY = {
			add_stability = -0.1
		}
	}
}

			ott_decrease_revolt_risk = yes
		}

	desc = ottomans_liberal_events.21.d

		controls_state = 291
		owns_state = 676
		has_war_with = EGY
		has_democratic_government = yes
		has_country_flag = yasin_goes_yeet
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;Iraq REVOLTS AGAINST OTT"
		hidden_effect = {
			291 = { teleport_armies = { limit = { is_ally_with = ROOT } to_state = 350 } }
			676 = { teleport_armies = { limit = { is_ally_with = ROOT } to_state = 350 } }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_liberal_events.21 option ottomans_liberal_events.21.a"
		name = ottomans_liberal_events.21.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_character = IRQ_yasin_al_hashimi }
				IRQ_yasin_al_hashimi = { set_nationality = IRQ }
			}
		}
		IRQ = {
			hidden_effect = {
				transfer_technology_without_doctrines = yes
				IRQ_yasin_al_hashimi = {
					set_nationality = PREV
					promote_character = yes
					promote_to_field_marshal = yes
				}
			}
			activate_advisor = IRQ_taha_al_hashimi_sic
			transfer_state = 676
			transfer_state = 291
			IRQ_spawn_initial_units = yes
			declare_war_on = {
				target = OTT
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		EGY = { add_to_faction = IRQ }
	}
}

country_event = {	#Elections for the Provincial Assembly

	title = ottomans_sabahaddin_events.5.t
	desc = ottomans_sabahaddin_events.5.d
	picture = GFX_OTT_Sultan_Speech

	trigger = {
		OTT_ottomans_have_post_defeat_content = no
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottomans_sabahaddin_events.6 days = 100 }
			country_event = { id = ottomans_liberal_events.18 days = 300 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_sabahaddin_events.5 option ottomans_sabahaddin_events.5.a"
		name = ottomans_sabahaddin_events.5.a
		ai_chance = { base = 66 }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		### Return Conservative votes to opposition
		subtract_from_variable = { con_sup_deputies = 30 tooltip = con_opp_tt }

		### Return Liberal votes to opposition
		subtract_from_variable = { ind_sup_deputies = 15 tooltip = ind_opp_tt }

		### Calculate coalition strength
		OTT_calc_coalition_strength = yes
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_sabahaddin_events.5 option ottomans_sabahaddin_events.5.b"
		name = ottomans_sabahaddin_events.5.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCLIB }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCCON }
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = ottomans_sabahaddin_events.7.a
		ai_chance = { base = 66 }
		add_political_power = 20
		676 = {
			ott_increase_revolt_risk = yes
		}
		291 = {
			ott_increase_revolt_risk = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_sabahaddin_events.7 option ottomans_sabahaddin_events.7.b"
		name = ottomans_sabahaddin_events.7.b
		ai_chance = { base = 33 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottomans_sabahaddin_events.8 days = 10 }
		}
		add_political_power = 10
		676 = {
			ott_increase_revolt_risk = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_sabahaddin_events.7 option ottomans_sabahaddin_events.7.c"
		name = ottomans_sabahaddin_events.7.c
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottomans_sabahaddin_events.8 days = 10 }
		}
		add_political_power = -30
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_sabahaddin_events.7 option ottomans_sabahaddin_events.7.e"
		name = ottomans_sabahaddin_events.7.e
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		add_war_support = 0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottomans_sabahaddin_events.8 days = 10 }
		}
		add_political_power = -75
		### Add Arab Nationalist votes in favour
		add_to_variable = { nat_ara_sup_deputies = 40 tooltip = nat_ara_sup_tt }

		### Calculate coalition strength
		OTT_calc_coalition_strength = yes
	}
}

country_event = {	#The TPC Affair
	id = ottomans_sabahaddin_events.11
	title = ottomans_sabahaddin_events.11.t
	desc = ottomans_sabahaddin_events.11.d
	picture = GFX_OTT_Oil2

	trigger = {
		OTT_ottomans_have_post_defeat_content = no
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_sabahaddin_events.11 option ottomans_sabahaddin_events.11.a"
		name = ottomans_sabahaddin_events.11.a
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_sabahaddin_events.11 option ottomans_sabahaddin_events.11.b"
		name = ottomans_sabahaddin_events.11.b
		add_resource = {
			type = oil
			amount = 20
			state = 676
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_war_with = OTT }
				num_of_factories > 35
				is_subject = no
				has_socialist_government = no
				any_owned_state = {
					is_coastal = yes
				}
			}
			country_event = ottomans_economy_events.7
		}
		if = {
			limit = { OTT_has_centralist_government = no }
			### Return Turkish nationalist votes to opposition
			subtract_from_variable = { nat_tur_sup_deputies = 30 tooltip = nat_tur_opp_tt }

			### Calculate coalition strength
			OTT_calc_coalition_strength = yes
		}
	}
}

		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = -0.2
		}

		add_to_variable = {
			var = odf_deputies
			value = ohf_deputies
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = ohf_deputies
			value = 0
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = odf_deputies
			value = 80
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = nat_tur_deputies
			value = 80
		}

		clamp_variable = {
			var = odf_deputies
			min = 0
			max = 500
		}

		### Calculate coalition strength
		OTT_calc_coalition_strength = yes
	}
}

		OTT_ottomans_have_post_defeat_content = no
	}

			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no
			name = TUR_military_government
			long_name = TUR_military_government_long
		}
		end_coalition = yes
		hidden_effect = { TUR_fevzi_cakmak = { set_nationality = ROOT } }
		activate_advisor = TUR_fevzi_cakmak_sic
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottomans_fevzi_events.1 days = 3 }
			country_event = { id = ottomans_fevzi_events.6 days = 14 }
			news_event = ottomans_news_events.3
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = EGY
						is_core_of = SUD
						is_core_of = ARM
						is_core_of = LBA
						is_core_of = TRP
						is_core_of = YEM
						is_core_of = HEJ
					}
				}
				clear_occupy_state = yes
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = ott_military_purge
		load_focus_tree = ottoman_fevzi_coup_focus
		complete_national_focus = OTT_State_of_Emergency
		set_stability = 0.6
		OTT_remove_kemalist_ideas = yes
	}
}

###############

add_namespace = ottomans_news_events

# Mustafa Kemal Seizes Power in the Ottoman Empire
news_event = {
	id = ottomans_news_events.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_news_events.1" }
	title = ottomans_news_events.1.t
	desc = ottomans_news_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_OTT_kemal_power

	major = yes
	fire_for_sender = no
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { wants_world_news = yes } #Global news event

	option = {
		name = ottomans_news_events.1.a
	}
}

# Prince Sabahattin Appointed Grand Vizier
news_event = {
	id = ottomans_news_events.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottomans_news_events.4" }
	title = ottomans_news_events.4.t

	desc = {
		text = ottomans_news_events.4.d.kemal_dead
		trigger = {
			NOT = { TUR = { has_character = TUR_mustafa_kemal_ataturk } }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ottomans_news_events.4.d.kemal_out
		trigger = {
			TUR = { has_character = TUR_mustafa_kemal_ataturk }
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_news_event_OTT_sabahaddin

	major = yes
	fire_for_sender = no
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { wants_world_news = yes } #Global news event

	option = {
		name = ottomans_news_events.4.a
	}
}
